Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Override with: `--compliance [strict|standard|light|exempt]`\"\n\n**Note**: The machine-readable header (Section 0) is for telemetry/A/B testing. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical feature)\n-> Context loaded before editing\n-> Downstream impacts checked\n-> Direct test execution\n```\n\n### LIGHT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"fix typo in README\"\n\n-> Classified as LIGHT (trivial classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n\n    Args:\n        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n\n    Returns:\n        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    if step_graph_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Step Graph Design\\n\\n\" + step_graph_content.strip())\n\n    if models_gates_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Models and Gates Design\\n\\n\" + models_gates_content.strip())\n\n    if prompts_executor_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n\n    return assembled\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> Exits cleanly with code 0.\n\n    Args:\n        config_cli_name: CLI name being portified (used in instructions).\n        workdir: Working directory where phase2-approval.yaml will be written.\n        step_results: List of PortifyStepResult objects from Phase 2 steps.\n                      If None, skips gate-pass validation.\n        _exit: If True (default), calls sys.exit(0). Set False in tests.\n\n    Raises:\n        PortifyValidationError: If blocking gates have not passed or portify-spec.md\n                                is missing or has an empty step_mapping section.\n    \"\"\"\n    # *args / **kwargs: Forwarded to *fn*.\n   163→\n   164→    Returns:\n   165→        The return value of *fn*.\n   166→\n   167→    Raises:\n   168→        TimeoutError: If *fn* does not complete within *timeout_s* seconds.\n   169→    \"\"\"\n   170→    with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as pool:\n   171→        future = pool.submit(fn, *args, **kwargs)\n   172→        try:\n   173→            return future.result(timeout=timeout_s)\n   174→        except concurrent.futures.TimeoutError:\n   175→            raise TimeoutError(\n   176→                f\"Operation timed out after {timeout_s}s\"\n   177→            )\n   178→\n   179→\n   180→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   181→# _determine_status()\n   182→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   183→\n   184→\n   185→def _determine_status(\n   186→    exit_code: int,\n   187→    timed_out: bool,\n   188→    stdout: str = \"\",\n   189→    artifact_path: Optional[Path] = None,\n   190→) -> PortifyStatus:\n   191→    \"\"\"Classify a step outcome from exit code, EXIT_RECOMMENDATION, and artifact.\n   192→\n   193→    Classification rules (priority order):\n   194→      1. exit 124 (or timed_out=True)  → TIMEOUT\n   195→      2. exit non-zero                 → ERROR\n   196→      3. exit 0 + marker + artifact    → PASS\n   197→      4. exit 0 + no marker + artifact → PASS_NO_SIGNAL  (triggers retry)\n   198→      5. exit 0 + artifact, no result  → PASS_NO_REPORT  (no retry)\n   199→      6. exit 0 + no artifact          → PASS_NO_REPORT\n   200→    \"\"\"\n   201→    if timed_out or exit_code == EXIT_CODE_TIMEOUT:\n   202→        return PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT\n   203→\n   204→    if exit_code != 0:\n   205→        return PortifyStatus.ERROR\n   206→\n   207→    # exit 0 paths\n   208→    has_marker = EXIT_RECOMMENDATION_MARKER in stdout\n   209→    artifact_exists = artifact_path is not None and Path(artifact_path).exists()\n   210→\n   211→    if has_marker and artifact_exists:\n   212→        return PortifyStatus.PASS\n   213→\n   214→    if not has_marker and artifact_exists:\n   215→        return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL  # triggers retry\n   216→\n   217→    # No artifact (or no result file) → no retry\n   218→    return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n   219→\n   220→\n   221→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   222→# Return contract helpers (T03.10)\n   223→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   224→\n   225→\n   226→def _build_resume_command(step_id: str, cli_name: str = \"portify\") -> str:\n   227→    \"\"\"Build the exact CLI command string for resuming from a step.\"\"\"\n   228→    return f\"superclaude cli-portify run --resume {step_id}\"\n   229→\n   230→\n   231→def _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps: list[PortifyStep]) -> int:\n   232→    \"\"\"Calculate suggested_resume_budget = remaining_steps_count * 25.\n   233→\n   234→    remaining = steps with PENDING or INCOMPLETE status.\n   235→    \"\"\"\n   236→    remaining = sum(\n   237→        1 for s in steps\n   238→        if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)\n   239→    )\n   240→    return remaining * 25\n   241→\n   242→\n   243→def _emit_return_contract(\n   244→    workdir: Path,\n   245→    outcome: PortifyOutcome,\n   246→    steps: list[PortifyStep],\n   247→    completed_steps: list[str],\n   248→    resume_from_step_id: str = \"\",\n   249→) -> Path:\n   250→    \"\"\"Emit return-contract.yaml to the workdir on ALL outcome paths (SC-011).\n   251→\n   252→    Returns the path to the emitted file.\n   253→    \"\"\"\n   254→    remaining_steps = [s.step_id for s in steps if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)]\n   255→    resume_command = _build_resume_command(resume_from_step_id) if resume_from_step_id else \"\"\n   256→    suggested_budget = _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps)\n   257→\n   258→    contract = {\n   259→        \"outcome\": outcome.value,\n   260→        \"completed_steps\": completed_steps,\n   261→        \"remaining_steps\": remaining_steps,\n   262→        \"resume_command\": \"return-contract.yaml\"\n   268→    with open(contract_path, \"w\") as fh:\n   269→        yaml.safe_dump(contract, fh, default_flow_style=False)\n   270→    return contract_path\n   271→\n   272→\n   273→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   274→# PortifyExecutor\n   275→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   276→\n   277→\n   278→class PortifyExecutor:\n   279→    \"\"\"Sequential pipeline executor for CLI Portify.\n   280→\n   281→    Usage:\n   282→        executor = PortifyExecutor(steps, workdir, Optional[Callable[[PortifyStep], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n   295→    ) -> None:\n   296→        \"\"\"\n   297→        Args:\n   298→            steps: Ordered list of steps in registered order.\n   299→            workdir: Working directory for artifacts and return contract.\n   300→            dry_run: If True, filter execution to DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES only.\n   301→            resume_from: Step ID to resume from (skip all prior steps).\n   302→            turn_budget: Total Claude-invocation budget (TurnLedger).\n   303→            step_runner: Optional callable (step) -> (exit_code, stdout, timed_out).\n   304→                         Used for testing; real runs use subprocess.\n   305→        \"\"\"\n   306→        self.steps = steps\n   307→        self.workdir = workdir\n   308→        self.dry_run = dry_run\n   309→        self.resume_from = resume_from\n   310→        self._ledger = TurnLedger(total_budget=turn_budget)\n   311→        self._step_runner = step_runner\n   312→        self._interrupted: bool = False\n   313→        self._completed_steps: list[str] = []\n   314→        self._step_results: dict[str, PortifyStepResult] = {}\n   315→\n   316→        # Signal handler integration points (T03.04 / T03.09)\n   317→        self._prev_sigint: Optional[Callable] = None\n   318→        self._prev_sigterm: Optional[Callable] = None\n   319→\n   320→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   321→    # Signal handling (T03.09)\n   322→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   323→\n   324→    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n   325→        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n   326→        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n   327→            self._interrupted = True\n   328→\n   329→        try:\n   330→            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n   331→            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n   332→        except (OSError, ValueError):\n   333→            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n   334→            pass\n   335→\n   336→    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n   337→        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n   338→        try:\n   339→            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n   340→                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n   341→            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n   342→                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n   343→        except (OSError, ValueError):\n   344→            pass\n   345→\n   346→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   347→    # Step filtering\n   348→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   349→\n   350→    def _should_execute(self, step: PortifyStep) -> bool:\n   351→        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n   352→        if self.dry_run:\n   353→            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n   354→        return True\n   355→\n   356→    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n   357→        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n   358→        return not resume_started\n   359→\n   360→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   361→    # Step execution\n   362→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   363→\n   364→    def _execute_step(self, step: PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n   365→        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n   366→        if self._step_runner is not None:\n   367→            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n   368→        else:\n   369→            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n   370→            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n   371→\n   372→        artifact_path = step.output_file\n   373→        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n   374→        self._ledger.consume(1)\n   375→\n   376→        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n   377→        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n   378→            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n   379→                if self._step_runner is not None:\n   380→                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n   381→                else:\n   382→                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n   383→                self._ledger.consume(1)\n   384→                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n   385→\n   386→        return status\n   387→\n   388→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   389→    # Main execution loop\n   390→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   391→\n   392→    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n   393→        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n   394→        self._install_signal_handlers()\n   395→        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n   396→        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n   397→\n   398→        try:\n   399→            for step in self.steps:\n   400→                # Check for interrupt before each step\n   401→                if self._interrupted:\n   402→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   403→                    break\n   404→\n   405→                # Resume skip logic\n   406→                if not resume_started:\n   407→                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n   408→                        resume_started = True\n   409→                    else:\n   410→                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n   411→                        continue\n   412→\n   413→                # Dry-run filtering\n   414→                if not self._should_execute(step):\n   415→                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n   416→                    continue\n   417→\n   418→                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n   419→                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n   420→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n   421→                    break\n   422→\n   423→                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n   424→                status = self._execute_step(step)\n   425→                step.status = status\n   426→\n   427→                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n   428→                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n   429→                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n   430→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n   431→                    break\n   432→                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n   433→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n   434→                    break\n   435→\n   436→                # Check interrupt after step completes\n   437→                if self._interrupted:\n   438→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   439→                    break\n   440→\n   441→        finally:\n   442→            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n   443→            # models_gates_content: str,\n   848→    prompts_executor_content: str,\n   849→) -> str:\n   850→    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n   851→\n   852→    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n   853→    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n   854→\n   855→    Args:\n   856→        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n   857→        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n   858→        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n   859→\n   860→    Returns:\n   861→        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n   862→    \"\"\"\n   863→    sections: list[str] = []\n len(matches) > 1:\n   883→        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n   884→        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n   885→            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n   886→\n   887→    return assembled\n   888→\n   889→\n   890→def execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n   891→    config_cli_name: str,\n   892→ First iteration uses 1.0 budget\n        engine.submit(IterationResult(iteration=1, unaddressed_criticals=2))\n        guard.record_spend(1.0)\n\n        # Check budget before second iteration — only 0.5 left, not enough\n        assert not engine.check_budget(1.0)\n        engine.escalate_budget()\n\n        assert engine.is_done\n        assert engine.state == ConvergenceState.ESCALATED\n        final = engine.result()\n        assert final.escalation_reason == EscalationReason.BUDGET_EXHAUSTED\n\n    def test_no_budget_guard_always_passes(self):\n        \"\"\"Without a budget guard, check_budget always returns True.\"\"\"\n        engine = ConvergenceEngine(max_iterations=3)\n        assert engine.check_budget(100.0)\n\n    def test_budget_guard_sufficient(self):\n        guard = SimpleBudgetGuard(total_budget=10.0, per_iteration_cost=1.0)\n        engine = ConvergenceEngine(max_iterations=3, budget_guard=guard)\n        assert engine.check_budget(1.0)\n\n\nclass TestUserRejection:\n\n    def test_user_rejection_escalates(self):\n        engine = ConvergenceEngine(max_iterations=3)\n        engine.submit(IterationResult(iteration=1, unaddressed_criticals=0))\n        # (8 + 7 + 9 + 6) / 4 = 7.5\n        assert result.overall_score == pytest.approx(7.5, abs=0.01)\n\n    def test_overall_score_empty(self):\n        result = IterationResult()\n        assert result.overall_score == 0.0\n\n    def test_partial_scores(self):\n        result = IterationResult(\n            quality_scores={\"clarity\": 8.0, \"completeness\": 6.0}\n        )\n        # If skills_root is provided, search for matching subdirectories.\n         - Exact match → return it.\n         - Partial match (multiple) → raise AmbiguousPathError.\n         - No match → raise InvalidPathError.\n      4. If no skills_root, treat name_or_path as a literal path.\n\n    Raises:\n        InvalidPathError: Path found but no SKILL.md present.\n        AmbiguousPathError: Partial name matches multiple skill directories.\n    \"\"\"\n    from .models import AmbiguousPathError, InvalidPathError\n\n    p = Path(name_or_path).resolve()\n\n    # Direct path resolution\n    if p.exists():\n        if p.is_file() and p.name == \"SKILL.md\":\n            return p.parent\n        if p.is_dir():\n            if not (p / \"SKILL.md\").exists():\n                raise InvalidPathError(str(p))\n            return p\n        raise InvalidPathError(str(p))\n\n    # Search under skills_root\n    if skills_root and skills_root.exists():\n        name = Path(name_or_path).name\n        candidates = [\n            d for d in skills_root.iterdir()\n            if d.is_dir() and name.lower() in d.name.lower()\n        ]\n        if len(candidates) == 1:\n            candidate = candidates[0]\n            if not (candidate / \"SKILL.md\").exists():\n                raise InvalidPathError(str(candidate))\n            return candidate\n        elif len(candidates) > 1:\n            from .models import AmbiguousPathError\n            raise AmbiguousPathError(str(name), [str(c) for c in candidates])\n        # No match under skills_root → fall through to not-found\n\n    raise InvalidPathError(str(p))\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T02.02: CLI Name Derivation\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef derive_cli_name(workflow_path: Path, explicit_name: Optional[str] = None) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Derive the CLI module name from a workflow path.\n\n    If explicit_name is provided, it is used directly (bypasses derivation).\n    Otherwise, derives from the workflow directory name by:\n      1. Stripping 'sc-' prefix\n      2. Stripping '-protocol' suffix\n      3. Normalizing to kebab-case\n\n    Raises:\n        DerivationFailedError: If derivation yields an empty string and no\n                               explicit_name was provided.\n    \"\"\"\n    from .models import DerivationFailedError\n\n    if explicit_name:\n        return explicit_name\n    return _derive_name_from_path(workflow_path)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T02.03: Collision Detection\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _check_collision(derived_name: str, config: PortifyConfig) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Check if derived CLI name collides with an existing module.\n\n    Returns list of error strings (empty if no collision).\n\n    A collision is blocked unless the existing module's __init__.py contains\n    portification markers ('Generated by' or 'Portified from').\n    \"\"\"\n    from .utils import is_portified_module\n\n    errors: list[str] = []\n\n    # Check known reserved CLI module names\n    normalized = derived_name.replace(\"-\", \"_\")\n    if derived_name in _KNOWN_CLI_MODULES or normalized in _KNOWN_CLI_MODULES:\n        errors.append(\n            f\"CLI name '{derived_name}' collides with existing module \"\n            f\"'{normalized}' — use --name to choose a different name\"\n        )\n        return errors\n\n    # Check filesystem collision under src/superclaude/cli/\n    cli_root = _find_cli_root(config)\n    if cli_root is None:\n        return errors\n\n    candidate = cli_root / normalized\n    if candidate.exists():\n        init_py = candidate / \"__init__.py\"\n        if init_py.exists() and is_portified_module(init_py):\n            # Overwrite allowed\n            return errors\n        errors.append(\n            f\"CLI name '{derived_name}' collides with existing module at \"\n            f\"{candidate} — use --name to choose a different name, or \"\n            \"add portification marker to __init__.py to allow overwrite\"\n        )\n\n    return errors\n\n\ndef _find_cli_root(config: PortifyConfig) -> Optional[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Find the src/superclaude/cli/ root for collision checking.\"\"\"\n    # Walk up from workflow_path to find the cli directory\n    search = config.workflow_path\n    for _ in range(10):\n        candidate = search / \"src\" / \"superclaude\" / \"cli\"\n        if candidate.exists():\n            return candidate\n        parent = search.parent\n        if parent == search:\n            break\n        search = parent\n    # Fallback: look relative to the package\n    import superclaude.cli\n    import importlib\n    try:\n        spec = importlib.util.find_spec(\"superclaude.cli\")\n        if spec and spec.submodule_search_locations:\n            return Path(list(spec.submodule_search_locations)[0])\n    except Exception:\n        pass\n    return None\n","numLines":330,"startLine":1,"totalLines":330}}}

sections for additive-only enforcement\n- generate_panel_report(): write panel-report.md with YAML frontmatter (FR-035)\n- prompt_user_review(): ask user to accept/reject the panel report\n- DOWNSTREAM_READINESS_THRESHOLD: 7.0 constant\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Optional\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.convergence import (\n    ConvergenceEngine,\n    ConvergenceResult,\n    ConvergenceState,\n    EscalationReason,\n    IterationResult,\n)\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.models import (\n    FailureClassification,\n    PortifyConfig,\n    PortifyStatus,\n    PortifyStepResult,\n)\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.process import PortifyProcess\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.utils import extract_sections, hash_section\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Constants\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nDOWNSTREAM_READINESS_THRESHOLD: float = 7.0\n\n_QUALITY_DIMENSIONS: tuple[str, ...] = (\n    \"clarity\",\n    \"completeness\",\n    \"testability\",\n    \"consistency\",\n)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Quality scoring\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef parse_quality_scores(content: str) -> dict[str, float]:\n    \"\"\"Extract quality scores from Claude output.\n\n    Supports two formats:\n      - Colon format:  ``clarity: 8.5``\n      - Table format:  ``| clarity | 8.5 |``\n\n    Returns:\n        Dict of {dimension: score}. Empty dict if no scores found.\n    \"\"\"\n    scores: dict[str, float] = {}\n\n    # Colon format: \"dimension: 8.5\"\n    colon_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"^\\s*(\" +  \"resume_command\": resume_command,\n        \"suggested_resume_budget\": suggested_budget,\n    }\n\n    workdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    contract_path = workdir / \"return-contract.yaml\"\n    with open(contract_path, \"w\") as fh:\n        yaml.safe_dump(contract, fh, default_flow_style=False)\n    return contract_path\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# PortifyExecutor\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass PortifyExecutor:\n    \"\"\"Sequential pipeline executor for CLI Portify.\n\n    Usage:\n        executor = PortifyExecutor(steps, workdir, dry_run=False)\n        outcome = executor.run()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        steps: list[PortifyStep],\n        workdir: Path,\n        *,\n        dry_run: bool = False,\n        resume_from: str = \"\",\n        turn_budget: int = 200,\n        step_runner: Optional[Callable[[PortifyStep], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"\n        Args:\n            steps: Ordered list of steps in registered order.\n            workdir: Working directory for artifacts and return contract.\n            dry_run: If True, filter execution to DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES only.\n            resume_from: Step ID to resume from (skip all prior steps).\n            turn_budget: Total Claude-invocation budget (TurnLedger).\n            step_runner: Optional callable (step) -> (exit_code, stdout, timed_out).\n                         Used for testing; real runs use subprocess.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.steps = steps\n        self.workdir = workdir\n        self.dry_run = dry_run\n        self.resume_from = resume_from\n        self._ledger = TurnLedger(total_budget=turn_budget)\n        self._step_runner = step_runner\n        self._interrupted: bool = False\n        self._completed_steps: list[str] = []\n        self._step_results: dict[str, PortifyStepResult] = {}\n\n        # Signal handler integration points (T03.04 / T03.09)\n        self._prev_sigint: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._prev_sigterm: Optional[Callable] = None\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Signal handling (T03.09)\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            pass\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step filtering\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _should_execute(self, step: PortifyStep) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n        if self.dry_run:\n            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n        return True\n\n    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n        return not resume_started\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step execution\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _execute_step(self, step: PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n        if self._step_runner is not None:\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n        else:\n            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n\n        artifact_path = step.output_file\n        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n        self._ledger.consume(1)\n\n        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n                if self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main execution loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n\n    Args:\n        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n\n    Returns:\n        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    if step_graph_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Step Graph Design\\n\\n\" + step_graph_content.strip())\n\n    if models_gates_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Models and Gates Design\\n\\n\" + models_gates_content.strip())\n\n    if prompts_executor_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n\n    return assembled\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) ->  \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.SPECIFICATION,\n        \"timeout_s\": 600,\n        \"retry_limit\": 1,\n    },\n    \"prompts-executor-design\": {\n        \"step_id\": \"step_id\": \"user-review-p2\",\n        \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.USER_REVIEW,\n        \"timeout_s\": 0,\n        \"retry_limit\": 0,\n    },\n    # Phase 7: Release spec synthesis step (T07.04, R-051, NFR-001)\n    \"release-spec-synthesis\": {\n        \"step_id\": \"release-spec-synthesis\",\n        \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.SYNTHESIS,\n        \"timeout_s\": 900,\n        \"retry_limit\": 1,\n    },\n    # Phase 8: Panel review step — internal convergence loop, no outer retry (T08.06, AC-011, NFR-001)\n    \"panel-review\": {\n        \"step_id\": \"panel-review\",\n        \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.CONVERGENCE,\n        \"timeout_s\": 1200,\n        \"retry_limit\": 0,\n    },\n}\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T02.09: run_with_timeout() — enforce step-level time budgets (NFR-001)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_with_timeout(fn: Callable[..., _T], timeout_s: float, *args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> _T:\n    \"\"\"Run *fn* in a thread and raise TimeoutError if it exceeds *timeout_s* seconds.\n\n    Used to enforce:\n      - SC-001: validate_and_configure() ≤ 30 s\n      - SC-002: discover_components()     ≤ 60 s\n\n    Args:\n        fn: Callable to execute.\n        timeout_s: Maximum allowed wall-clock seconds.\n        *args / **kwargs: Forwarded to *fn*.\n\n    Returns:\n        The return value of *fn*.\n\n    Raises:\n        TimeoutError: If *fn* does not complete within *timeout_s* seconds.\n    \"\"\"\n    with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as pool:\n        future = pool.submit(fn, *args, **kwargs)\n        try:\n            return future.result(timeout=timeout_s)\n        except concurrent.futures.TimeoutError:\n            raise TimeoutError(\n                f\"Operation timed out after {timeout_s}s\"\n            )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# _determine_status()\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    timed_out: bool,\n    stdout: str = \"\",\n    artifact_path: Optional[Path] = None,\n) -> PortifyStatus:\n    \"\"\"Classify a step outcome from exit code, EXIT_RECOMMENDATION, and artifact.\n\n    Classification rules (priority order):\n      1. exit 124 (or timed_out=True)  → TIMEOUT\n      2. exit non-zero                 → ERROR\n      3. exit 0 + marker + artifact    → PASS\n      4. exit 0 + no marker + artifact → PASS_NO_SIGNAL  (triggers retry)\n      5. exit 0 + artifact, no result  → PASS_NO_REPORT  (no retry)\n      6. exit 0 + no artifact          → PASS_NO_REPORT\n    \"\"\"\n    if timed_out or exit_code == EXIT_CODE_TIMEOUT:\n        return PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return PortifyStatus.ERROR\n\n    # exit 0 paths\n    has_marker = EXIT_RECOMMENDATION_MARKER in stdout\n    artifact_exists = artifact_path is not None and Path(artifact_path).exists()\n\n    if has_marker and artifact_exists:\n        return PortifyStatus.PASS\n\n    if not has_marker and artifact_exists:\n        return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL  # triggers retry\n\n    # No artifact (or no result file) → no retry\n    return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Return contract helpers (T03.10)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _build_resume_command(step_id: str, cli_name: str = \"portify\") -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build the exact CLI command string for resuming from a step.\"\"\"\n    return f\"superclaude cli-portify run --resume {step_id}\"\n\n\ndef _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps: list[PortifyStep]) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Calculate suggested_resume_budget = remaining_steps_count * 25.\n\n    remaining = steps with PENDING or INCOMPLETE status.\n    \"\"\"\n    remaining = sum(\n        1 for s in steps\n        if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)\n    )\n    return remaining * 25\n\n\ndef _emit_return_contract(\n    workdir: Path,\n    outcome: PortifyOutcome,\n    steps: list[PortifyStep],\n    completed_steps: list[str],\n    resume_from_step_id: str = \"\",\n) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Emit return-contract.yaml to the workdir on ALL outcome paths (SC-011).\n\n    Returns the path to the emitted file.\n    \"\"\"\n    remaining_steps = [s.step_id for s in steps if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)]\n    resume_command = _build_resume_command(resume_from_step_id) if resume_from_step_id else \"\"\n    suggested_budget = _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps)\n\n    contract = {\n        \"outcome\": outcome.value,\n        \"completed_steps\": completed_steps,\n        \"remaining_steps\": remaining_steps,\n        \"resume_command\": resume_command,\n        \"suggested_resume_budget\": suggested_budget,\n    }\n\n    workdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    contract_path = workdir / \"return-contract.yaml\"\n    with open(contract_path, \"w\") as fh:\n        yaml.safe_dump(contract, fh, default_flow_style=False)\n    return contract_path\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# PortifyExecutor\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass PortifyExecutor:\n    \"\"\"Sequential pipeline executor for CLI Portify.\n\n    Usage:\n        executor = PortifyExecutor(steps, workdir, dry_run=False)\n        outcome = executor.run()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        steps: list[PortifyStep],\n        workdir: Path,\n        *,\n        dry_run: bool = False,\n        resume_from: str = \"\",\n        turn_budget: int = 200,\n        step_runner: Optional[Callable[[PortifyStep], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"\n        Args:\n            steps: Ordered list of steps in registered order.\n            workdir: Working directory for artifacts and return contract.\n            dry_run: If True, filter execution to DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES only.\n            resume_from: Step ID to resume from (skip all prior steps).\n            turn_budget: Total Claude-invocation budget (TurnLedger).\n            step_runner: Optional callable (step) -> (exit_code, stdout, timed_out).\n                         Used for testing; real runs use subprocess.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.steps = steps\n        self.workdir = workdir\n        self.dry_run = dry_run\n        self.resume_from = resume_from\n        self._ledger = TurnLedger(total_budget=turn_budget)\n        self._step_runner = step_runner\n        self._interrupted: bool = False\n        self._completed_steps: list[str] = []\n        self._step_results: dict[str, PortifyStepResult] = {}\n\n        # Signal handler integration points (T03.04 / T03.09)\n        self._prev_sigint: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._prev_sigterm: Optional[Callable] = None\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Signal handling (T03.09)\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            pass\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step filtering\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _should_execute(self, step: PortifyStep) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n        if self.dry_run:\n            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n        return True\n\n    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n        return not resume_started\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step execution\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _execute_step(self, step: PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n        if self._step_runner is not None:\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n        else:\n            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n\n        artifact_path = step.output_file\n        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n        self._ledger.consume(1)\n\n        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n                if self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main execution loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. Empty dict if no scores found.\n    \"\"\"\n    scores: dict[str, float] = {}\n\n    # Colon format: \"dimension: 8.5\"\n    colon_pattern = re.compile(\n        r\"^\\s*(\" + \"|\".join(_QUALITY_DIMENSIONS) + r\")\\s*:\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*$\",\n        re.IGNORECASE | re.MULTILINE,\n    )\n    for m in colon_pattern.finditer(content):\n        dim = m.group(1).lower()\n        scores[dim] = float(m.group(2))\n\n    # Table format: \"| clarity | 8.5 |\"\n    if not scores:\n        table_pattern = re.compile(\n            r\"\\|\\s*(\" + \"|\".join(_QUALITY_DIMENSIONS) + r\")\\s*\\|\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*\\|\",\n            re.IGNORECASE,\n        )\n        for m in table_pattern.finditer(content):\n            dim = m.group(1).lower()\n            scores[dim] = float(m.group(2))\n\n    return scores\n\n\ndef compute_overall_score(scores: dict[str, float]) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Return the mean of the 4 quality dimensions (missing dimensions = 0).\"\"\"\n    if not scores:\n        return 0.0\n    total = sum(scores.get(d, 0.0) for d in _QUALITY_DIMENSIONS)\n    return total / 4.0\n\n\ndef check_downstream_readiness(overall: float) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Return True if overall score meets the downstream readiness threshold (FR-034).\"\"\"\n    return overall >= DOWNSTREAM_READINESS_THRESHOLD\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Critical counting\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef count_unaddressed_criticals(content: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Count CRITICAL findings NOT marked [RESOLVED] or [INCORPORATED] or [DISMISSED].\n\n    A CRITICAL is unaddressed when the line contains 'CRITICAL' but does NOT\n    start with a resolved/dismissed marker.\n    \"\"\"\n    count = 0\n    for line in content.splitlines():\n        stripped = line.strip()\n        if \"CRITICAL\" not in stripped.upper():\n            continue\n        upper = stripped.upper()\n        if upper.startswith(\"[RESOLVED]\") or upper.startswith(\"[INCORPORATED]\") or upper.startswith(\"[DISMISSED]\"):\n            continue\n        count += 1\n    return count\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Section hashing\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef capture_section_hashes(content: str) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Capture hashes of all ## sections in content.\n\n    Returns:\n        Dict of {section_title: sha256_hex}.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections = extract_sections(content)\n    return {title: hash_section(body) for title, body in sections.items()}\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Panel report generation\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef generate_panel_report(\n    convergence_result: ConvergenceResult,\n    quality_scores: dict[str, float],\n    overall_score: float,\n    downstream_ready: bool,\n    output_path: Path,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write panel-report.md with YAML frontmatter and human-readable sections.\n\n    The frontmatter includes all machine-readable fields required by FR-035 and SC-010:\n      terminal_state, iteration_count, overall, downstream_ready,\n      individual quality dimensions, and escalation_reason (if escalated).\n\n    Args:\n        convergence_result: Final convergence engine result.\n        quality_scores: Dict of dimension scores.\n        overall_score: Pre-computed overall (mean of 4 dimensions).\n        downstream_ready: Whether the overall threshold was met.\n        output_path: Where to write panel-report.md.\n    \"\"\"\n    terminal_state = convergence_result.state.value.lower()\n    iteration_count = convergence_result.iterations_completed\n\n    # --- YAML frontmatter ---\n    fm_lines = [\n        \"---\",\n        f\"terminal_state: {terminal_state}\",\n        f\"iteration_count: {iteration_count}\",\n        f\"overall: {overall_score}\",\n        f\"downstream_ready: {'true' if downstream_ready else 'false'}\",\n    ]\n\n    for dim in _QUALITY_DIMENSIONS:\n        if dim in quality_scores:\n            fm_lines.append(f\"{dim}: {quality_scores[dim]}\")\n\n    if convergence_result.escalation_reason is not None:\n        fm_lines.append(f\"escalation_reason: {convergence_result.escalation_reason.value}\")\n\n    fm_lines.append(\"---\")\n    fm_lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # --- Human-readable body ---\n    body_lines: list[str] = []\n\n    body_lines += [\n        \"## Convergence Summary\",\n        \"\",\n        f\"**Terminal State**: {terminal_state.upper()}\",\n        f\"**Iterations Completed**: {iteration_count}\",\n    ]\n\n    if convergence_result.escalation_reason is not None:\n        body_lines.append(f\"**Escalation Reason**: {convergence_result.escalation_reason.value}\")\n\n    body_lines += [\"\", \"## Quality Scores\", \"\"]\n    body_lines.append(\"| Dimension | Score |\")\n    body_lines.append(\"|-----------|-------|\")\n    for dim in _QUALITY_DIMENSIONS:\n        score = quality_scores.get(dim, 0.0)\n        body_lines.append(f\"| {dim} | {score} |\")\n    body_lines.append(f\"| **overall** | {overall_score} |\")\n\n    body_lines += [\n        \"\",\n        \"## Downstream Readiness\",\n        \"\",\n        f\"**downstream_ready**: {'true' if downstream_ready else 'false'}\",\n        \"\",\n        f\"Threshold: {DOWNSTREAM_READINESS_THRESHOLD} — \"\n        + (\"PASSED\" if downstream_ready else \"NOT MET\"),\n        \"\",\n    ]\n\n    content = \"\\n\".join(fm_lines + body_lines)\n    output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    output_path.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# User review prompt\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef prompt_user_review(artifact_path: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Ask the user whether to accept the panel report artifact.\n\n    Returns True if accepted, False if rejected/EOF/interrupt.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"\\n[Panel Review] Artifact produced: {artifact_path}\")\n    print(\"Accept and continue? [y/N] \", end=\"\", flush=True)\n    try:\n        response = input().strip().lower()\n    except (EOFError, KeyboardInterrupt):\n        return False\n    return response in (\"y\", \"yes\")\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# run_panel_review\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_panel_review(config: PortifyConfig) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the full panel-review step (Step 7, Phase 4).\n\n    Requires:\n        - ``config.results_dir / \"synthesized-spec.md\"`` (prior step artifact)\n        - ``config.results_dir / \"brainstorm-gaps.md\"``  (prior step artifact)\n\n    Produces:\n        - ``config.results_dir / \"panel-reviewed-spec.md\"``\n        - ``config.results_dir / \"panel-report.md\"``\n\n    Returns:\n        PortifyStepResult with step_name=\"panel-review\", step_number=7, phase=4,\n        gate_tier=\"STRICT\".\n    \"\"\"\n    from superclaude.cli.cli_portify.executor import STEP_REGISTRY\n\n    step_name = \"panel-review\"\n    step_number = 7\n    phase = 4\n    gate_tier = \"STRICT\"\n\n    results_dir = config.results_dir\n    if results_dir is None:\n        return PortifyStepResult(\n            step_name=step_name,\n            step_number=step_number,\n            phase=phase,\n            portify_status=PortifyStatus.FAIL,\n            failure_classification=FailureClassification.MISSING_ARTIFACT,\n            gate_tier=gate_tier,\n            error_message=\"No results_dir configured on PortifyConfig\",\n        )\n\n    # --- Check required prior artifacts ---\n    spec_path = results_dir / \"synthesized-spec.md\"\n    gaps_path = results_dir / \"brainstorm-gaps.md\"\n\n    if not spec_path.exists():\n        return PortifyStepResult(\n            step_name=step_name,\n            step_number=step_number,\n            phase=phase,\n            portify_status=PortifyStatus.FAIL,\n            failure_classification=FailureClassification.MISSING_ARTIFACT,\n            gate_tier=gate_tier,\n            error_message=f\"Required artifact missing: {spec_path}\",\n        )\n\n    if not gaps_path.exists():\n        return PortifyStepResult(\n            step_name=step_name,\n            step_number=step_number,\n            phase=phase,\n            portify_status=PortifyStatus.FAIL,\n            failure_classification=FailureClassification.MISSING_ARTIFACT,\n            gate_tier=gate_tier,\n            error_message=f\"Required artifact missing: {gaps_path}\",\n        )\n\n    # --- Build output paths ---\n    results_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    output_artifact = results_dir / \"panel-reviewed-spec.md\"\n    error_file = results_dir / \"panel-review.err\"\n    report_path = results_dir / \"panel-report.md\"\n\n    # --- Determine timeout from registry ---\n    timeout_s: int = STEP_REGISTRY.get(step_name, {}).get(\"timeout_s\", 1200)\n\n    # --- Build prompt ---\n    spec_content = spec_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    gaps_content = gaps_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    prompt = _build_panel_review_prompt(spec_content, gaps_content)\n\n    # --- Parse output ---\n    output_text = proc_result.stdout_text or \"\"\n    quality_scores = parse_quality_scores(output_text)\n    overall = compute_overall_score(quality_scores)\n    unaddressed = count_unaddressed_criticals(output_text)\n\n    # --- Run convergence engine (internal loop, not outer retry) ---\n    engine = ConvergenceEngine(max_iterations=3)\n    engine.submit(IterationResult(\n        iteration=1,\n        unaddressed_criticals=unaddressed,\n        quality_scores=quality_scores,\n    ))\n    convergence_result = engine.result()\n\n    # --- User review gate (if not skipped) ---\n    if not config.skip_review:\n        accepted = prompt_user_review(str(output_artifact))\n        if not accepted:\n            return PortifyStepResult(\n                step_name=step_name,\n                step_number=step_number,\n                phase=phase,\n                portify_status=PortifyStatus.FAIL,\n                failure_classification=FailureClassification.USER_REJECTION,\n                gate_tier=gate_tier,\n                artifact_path=str(output_artifact),\n                error_message=\"User rejected panel review artifact\",\n                review_accepted=False,\n            )\n\n    return PortifyStepResult(\n        step_name=step_name,\n        step_number=step_number,\n        phase=phase,\n        portify_status=PortifyStatus.PASS,\n        gate_tier=gate_tier,\n        artifact_path=str(output_artifact),\n        iteration_timeout=timeout_s,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Internal helpers\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _build_panel_review_prompt(spec_content: str, gaps_content: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build the panel-review prompt for Claude.\"\"\"\n    return f\"\"\"You are conducting a final quality review of a CLI pipeline specification.\n\n## Synthesized Specification\n\n{spec_content}\n\n## Gap Analysis Findings\n\n{gaps_content}\n\n## Review Instructions\n\nReview the specification against the gap analysis findings.
